class=\"entry-header page-header\">\n\n\t\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title \">The Migrant Invasion of Europe: Get Ready for Riots and the Abolition of the White Race</h1>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"byline\"> <i class=\"fa fa-user fa-2x\"></i> <span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/author/admin/\">Admin</a></span></span><span class=\"posted-on\"><i class=\"fa fa-calendar\"></i> <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/the-migrant-invasion-of-europe-get-ready-for-riots-and-the-abolition-of-the-white-race/\" rel=\"bookmark\"><time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2017-03-04T12:03:05+00:00\">March 4, 2017</time><time class=\"updated\" datetime=\"2017-03-04T19:04:29+00:00\">March 4, 2017</time></a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"cat-links\"><i class=\"fa fa-folder-open-o\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/category/prose/\" rel=\"category tag\">Articles</a>\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\t\t<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><strong>By <span style=\"color: #800000;\"><em>LASHA DARKMOON</em></span></strong></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><em><strong>&#8220;Lasha Darkmoon explains why Angela Merkel has probably wrought greater damage to Germany and Europe as a whole than Hitler.&#8221; (Rixon Stewart, <a href=\"http://www.thetruthseeker.co.uk/?p=147992\">Truthseeker</a>)</strong></em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><strong>The material presented below, based on previous articles published in <em>The Occidental Observer</em>, will serve as a short introduction to an electrifying video which forms the centerpiece of this article. I am told the 19-minute video could be removed from YouTube any day soon. This is because of constant complaints about it from the Usual Suspects, particularly about the shockingly damning quote by Jewish activist Barbara Spectre which forms the climax of the video. \u00a0\u00a0</strong></p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-56193\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Merkel-Wilders-Tweet-1.jpg.pagespeed.ce.HlsUYUYe0l.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"636\" height=\"382\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Merkel-Wilders-Tweet-1.jpg 636w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Merkel-Wilders-Tweet-1-150x90.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Merkel-Wilders-Tweet-1-300x180.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Merkel-Wilders-Tweet-1-600x360.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 636px) 100vw, 636px\"/></p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #800000;\">GERMAN CHANCELLOR ANGELA MERKEL</span></h4>\n<p><strong>\u00a7 \u00a0&#8220;There will be riots in Germany soon&#8230; I always thought Merkel was a great leader&#8230; [but] what she&#8217;s done in Germany is insane, <em>insane</em>&#8230;&#8221; \u00a0\u2014 Donald Trump in video below, 13.35 ff.</strong></p>\n<p><strong>\u00a7 \u00a0\u201cMerkel is at the risk of an imminent mental breakdown and now represents a\u00a0<a href=\"http://macedoniaonline.eu/content/view/28760/54/\">danger to Germany</a>.\u201d \u2014 Hans-Joachim Maaz, top German psychiatrist and best-selling author</strong><span id=\"more-62036\"></span></p>\n<hr/>\n<p><strong>Consumed with Holocaust guilt and possessed by the demons of pathological altruism, German Chancellor Angela Merkel has handed over her country to the endless hordes of the Third World. \u201cLet them come . . . we can look after them all,\u201d she murmurs serenely, echoing the words of the altruists all over Europe bearing placards that scream: \u201c<a href=\"https://www.google.com/search?site=&amp;tbm=isch&amp;source=hp&amp;biw=1920&amp;bih=985&amp;q=refugees+welcome+banner&amp;oq=Refugees+welcome&amp;gs_l=img.1.2.0l10.9523.15592.0.23003.16.10.0.6.6.0.87.737.10.10.0....0...1ac.1.64.img..0.16.746.aWjhie-uib4#tbm=isch&amp;q=refugees+welcome\">REFUGEES WELCOME</a>!</strong></p>\n<p>Merkel is an interesting case history: the guilt-ridden, traumatized leader of a deeply traumatized nation. Her way of handling the migrant crisis in Germany is not so much a stupendous example of pathological altruism at work as a symbolic act of self-flagellation on behalf of the German people, all of them engaged in varying degrees of self-flagellation over the Holocaust.</p>\n<blockquote><p>\u201cThe culture of the Holocaust is destroying Germany, \u201d Brenton Sanderson\u00a0<strong><a href=\"http://www.theoccidentalobserver.net/2016/01/a-review-of-why-the-germans-why-the-jews-part-1/\">notes</a></strong>\u00a0in a thought-provoking 3-part article in the\u00a0<em>Occidental Observer</em>. \u201cEndlessly reinforced over decades by the intellectual and media elite, the notion that Germans and their descendants are responsible for \u201cthe single most evil event in human history\u201d has had such a demoralizing effect that millions fully support Angela Merkel\u2019s current attempt to destroy the ethnic basis of their nation.\u201d</p></blockquote>\n<p>To understand \u00a0these words is to grasp the root cause of Germany\u2019s suicidal approach to the migrant crisis. Letting Germany be destroyed, the entire ethnic basis of the nation expunged, can be seen for what it is:\u00a0<em>a collective act of atonement for the Holocaust</em>.</p>\n<p>I wrote this last year in an article \u2014 the situation, if anything, is even worse now:</p>\n<blockquote><p>Germany has accepted roughly\u00a0<strong><a href=\"http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/dec/08/germany-on-course-to-accept-one-million-refugees-in-2015\">1.5 million \u201crefugees\u201d last year</a></strong>, far more than any other country in Europe, with a predicted \u00a0<strong><a href=\"http://www.express.co.uk/news/world/636552/Migrant-crisis-Europe-four-million-refugees-2017\">4\u00a0million new asylum seekers</a></strong>\u00a0pouring into Europe in 2016, and <strong><a href=\"https://www.rt.com/news/328692-refugees-future-europe-germany/\">10 million more on the way</a></strong>. Many of these will end up in Germany. At this rate, it is widely predicted, there will soon not be a single white face left in Germany\u2014or indeed anywhere else in Europe. In 50 years time, Europe will not only be multicultural, much to the delight of\u00a0<strong><a href=\"http://renegadetribune.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/wpid-barbara-spectre-quote-e1441221823269.jpeg\">Jewish activist Barbara Spectre</a></strong>, it will also be multicolored.</p></blockquote>\n<p>Last year a Muslim political activist warned the Germans: \u201cWe will marry your daughters and\u00a0<strong><a href=\"http://www.zerohedge.com/news/2015-11-04/muslim-man-warns-germans-we-will-marry-your-daughters-and-conquer-you-births\">conquer you with births</a></strong>!\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cWhat\u2019s wrong with that?\u201d you might ask if you\u2019ve been infected by the virus of pathological altruism. Well, to start with, most well-balanced Europeans don\u2019t want to see their homelands invaded by unlimited numbers of foreigners from Africa, Asia and the Middle East. They maintain, quite rightly, \u201cWe\u2019re full up<strong>,\u00a0<a href=\"http://www.breitbart.com/london/2016/01/20/mainstream-tabloids-finally-wake-up-to-migrant-crisis/\">we\u2019re \u00a0stuffed</a>\u00a0</strong>to capacity<strong>!</strong>\u201d</p>\n<p>If Europe can be likened to the Titanic sinking beneath the waves, the last thing we can afford is to have more people piling on to the lifeboats.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">\u00a0\u2014 \u00a0\u00a7 \u00a0\u2014</p>\n<p><strong>Here is a Muslim</strong> on a YouTube video. Listen to his rant. You\u2019ll be hearing more talk like this soon. He\u2019s not going to kill us quickly and violently with\u00a0<em>bombs and box cutters</em>, he\u2019s going to kill us slowly and non-violently with\u00a0<em>birth rates!</em></p>\n<blockquote><p><strong>\u201cI am telling you honestly, Islam will come to Germany, whether you like it or not. Your daughter will wear a headscarf (hijab). Your son will wear a beard. Okay. And your daughter will marry a bearded man.</strong></p>\n<p><strong>We are reproducing faster and faster. You Germans are not getting any children. In the best case, you get two children. We make seven to eight children. Okay, mate? And then we take four wives each, we have 22 children!\u00a0 Maybe you Germans have one child and a dog, huh? And that\u2019s it!</strong></p>\n<p><strong>Listen, mate. This is not our fault, it\u2019s\u00a0<em>your</em>\u00a0fault. You exploited our countries, colonized our countries.</strong></p>\n<p><strong>And so Allah (blessed be his name), Almighty God will make it so that we will conquer you. Not with war, here in Germany, but with\u00a0<em>birth rates</em>, first and foremost!\u00a0 Secondly,\u00a0<em>we will marry your daughters!</em>\u00a0And your daughter will wear a Muslim headscarf!</strong></p>\n<p><strong>That\u2019s how it is, mate! Now you can get really mad! I can already see\u00a0<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=JquXlQTBWOo\">the hate in your eyes</a>!\u201d</strong></p></blockquote>\n<p>If you have time, check out this\u00a0<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6gyr5XsOufw\"><strong>4-minute video</strong></a>\u00a0of a young African bragging about how he and other Black immigrants are going to conquer Europe and impregnate every beautiful White woman they can. \u201cWe are taking Europe from the Europeans and they are too stupid to fight back,\u201d he gloats. (0.30). \u201cThey are going to pay us to conquer them and take their land.\u201d (1.20). He adds with a smile, \u201cWhat I look forward to most is the destruction of European womanhood.\u201d (1.30).</p>\n<p>Talking of the \u201cdestruction of European womanhood,\u201d take a quick look at\u00a0<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-3MvinY66r0&amp;oref=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3D-3MvinY66r0&amp;has_verified=1\"><strong>this 1-minute video clip</strong></a>. This will give you an insight into the unimaginable depravities to which German women are now being exposed after the invasion of the migrant body snatchers. Here is a migrant boasting in broken German about the gang rape of a young girl on a bunk bed, a virgin, seven of them jumping her at once. English subtitles:</p>\n<blockquote><p><strong>\u201cAdim switched off the light and f****d her. (0.14) \u2026 She cried after that, she couldn\u2019t go any longer. (0.45) \u2026 And we, like pigs we spit on her. Sperm and dirt all over her. We really got milked. (0.47) \u2026 DUDE, it was a virgin! And we DESTROYED her with seven guys, dude. (0.57).</strong></p></blockquote>\n<p>In the 19-minute video featured below I was astonished to see a young Muslim migrant in Germany point to his genital region and say: &#8220;I have a big problem down here. My balls are very big. The doctor says,<em> make sex with anyone, make anything!</em>&#8221; (17.05). A quick check on the internet will tell you that scrotal elephantiasis, also known as scrotal lymphedema , is a real problem for many people. It consists of a \u00a0massive enlargement of the scrotum due to thickening of tissue and accumulation of fluid. Here is a picture of a man with an enlarged <strong><a href=\"http://i2.cdn.cnn.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/130819134056-tlc-enlarged-scrotum-horizontal-large-gallery.jpg\">132-pound scrotum</a></strong>.</p>\n<p>OK, this is obviously an <strong><a href=\"https://www.centerforreconstructiveurology.org/other-disorders/scrotal-lymphedema/#.WLqksxLyii4\">affliction</a></strong> you wouldn&#8217;t want to inflict on your deadliest enemy, but here is a Muslim migrant in Germany who has evidently been told by his witch doctor that the only way to find relief for his condition is to go out and have sex with as many German women as possible \u2014 if necessary by raping them. &#8220;Make sex with anyone, <em>make anything</em>!&#8221; he is instructed.</p>\n<p>Truly, the mind boggles: mass rape as a cure for scrotal elephantiasis!</p>\n<p>And so it seems we\u2019re\u00a0 all on board now for a new Europe in which the inhabitants of Africa (population 1.2 billion) will be given every opportunity to relocate to Europe and interbreed with the White women they encounter there, mass-producing in the process a long assembly line of babies that are neither black nor white but some intermediate shade of color. Add to this multicultural brew the seething masses of Asia (4.4 billion) and the pullulating Muslim populations of the world\u00a0 (1.6 billion), and then wave placards saying \u201c<a href=\"http://l7.alamy.com/zooms/6f5a86a71dc644bd82822ef766dc172c/belfast-northern-ireland-uk-30th-aug-2015people-holding-refugees-welcome-f1w6db.jpg\"><strong>Refugees Welcome</strong></a><strong>!</strong>\u201d and \u201c<a href=\"http://www.usnews.com/cmsmedia/39/18/0fa83e2545b1b464320a77e1ccf1/150924-poland-editorial.jpg\"><strong>Welcome Lovely Humans</strong></a>!\u201d\u2014and what do you have?</p>\n<p>Answer:\u00a0<em>Hell on earth.</em></p>\n<blockquote><p><strong>I don\u2019t think Orwell foresaw this multicultural superstate. This is something new. All we can be sure of is that this Eurostan\u2014the new European superstate now in the making\u2014will be a multicultural dystopia rife with race wars, gang rapes, cheap foreign labor, widespread unemployment for the dispossessed White minority, bullying bosses, cowed workers, overflowing prisons, fatcat lawyers, psychotic politicians, police state surveillance, fabricated news items, false flag attacks, demoralized families, dysfunctional children, schools for morons, mass suicides, manufactured diseases, promoted perversions, drug addiction, gambling, prostitution, pornography, serial killers on the rampage, and nonstop mindless entertainment for the zombified masses.</strong></p>\n<p><strong>It will be a dog-eat-dog world of unimaginable cruelty. A nightmare horrorshow that neither Dante nor Hieronymus Bosch ever anticipated in their wildest dreams. If you\u2019re White and dispossessed in this New Dystopia, you\u2019re a dead man walking. Get ready for t</strong><em><strong>he Abolition of the White rac</strong>e</em>.</p></blockquote>\n<p>If you haven&#8217;t seen this video below, you should. It is incomparably the best video on the migrant crisis you are ever likely to see. If you&#8217;ve seen it already, watch it again and send it to all your friends on Facebook and elsewhere.</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #800000;\">VIDEO : 19:32 mins</span></h4>\n<p><iframe width=\"648\" height=\"365\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/Sirj6qNLAEU?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>\n<!-- Simple Share Buttons Adder (6.3.4) simplesharebuttons.com --><div class=\"ssba ssba-wrap\"><div style=\"text-align:center\">Like this? class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/the-migrant-invasion-of-europe-get-ready-for-riots-and-the-abolition-of-the-white-race/#comment-948437\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>It\u2019s midnight. A hound howls in the distance as a cold wind journeys across the moors to make its way through a long forgotten graveyard. Light from a Darkmoon casts dim shadows that play across an open grave. Slowly, the casket lid stirs, causing dust to weep through widened cracks in dry, ancient wood. Rusty hinges creak, groaning their protest to a slowly opening coffin lid concealing a tragic figure of political consequences. </p>\n<p>Dead bones crack and dusty bits of uniform return to the grave as the corpse of a dead rebel rises slowly from the casket. Yellowed, sightless eyes shrunken into bottomless sockets stare blankly from above a sardonic grin, stretched tightly across a brown skull covered with mold; its ghastly visage makes the stomach churn. </p>\n<p>Rotting flesh crumbles from an empty sleeve as a boney finger of white stretches forth, pointing towards eternity. The mouth opens, fauna from the grave creeps forth accompanied by a hollow laugh from a ghostly past that echoes across the moors . . . It\u2019s time once again for Arch Stanton\u2019s &#8211; Theater ~ Of ~ The ~ Absurd. Tonight\u2019s episode is brought to you by the makers of RJF soap, the soap that makes a body Talmedically pure.</p>\n<p>Welcome fellow goyim. Tonight we travel back through the gray mists of time to enjoy yet more terrifyingly anti-semitic, black, SS humor as we present another episode from The Kremasign Theater\u2019s ongoing saga of Nhadzee atrocities. </p>\n<p>And now, from the hit album: \u201cDon\u2019t bash that Jew\u2019s brains out, hand me the Zyklon B,\u201d Harry Heydrich &#8211; Demonic Dealer of Death! </p>\n<p>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~</p>\n<p>Kookenwald Death Camp: He walks again by night with his faithful seeing-eye Schnauzer, Blindie, dogging Jews at every turn (ruff, ruff). Out of the fog, into the oven\u2019s smoke \u2013 relentlessly, ruthlessly, (I know Ruth was in the Bible, but I can\u2019t remember where) for his evening meeting with the incredibly unbelievable. </p>\n<p>At the corner of Himmelstra\u00dfe and Arbeit Macht Frei he turns right. At Arbeit Macht Frei and Himmelstra\u00dfe he turns left and walks into a gray cement building (Ow!) He steps inside to climb the thirteen steps to his office of fear and terror. Walking in, he\u2019s ready for horror! He\u2019s ready for torture! He\u2019s ready for blood! He\u2019s Harry Heydrich \u2013 Demonic Dealer of Death!   </p>\n<p>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~</p>\n<p>According to the clavicle clock on the wall, it was late afternoon at the death camp when I flipped on the human finger switch that put a more literal angle on the Judens\u2019 infamous, light-fingered nature. I had just finished my usual day piling corpses 800 meters into the sky before turning them into canned meat for the troops. The sign over the camp\u2019s entrance tallied the score, \u201cOver Six Million Served.\u201d</p>\n<p>Sitting down at a desk made of human bones, I put my hob-nailed jackboots up on the shrunken head that served as a footstool and lit a rauche to help compose my thoughts. Reflecting on the utter absurdity of giving prisoners haircuts and identifying tattoos only to march them off to the gas chambers a few moments later, I reasoned the SS could save time, not to mention quite a few Reichmarks, by eliminating the lengthy process. There might even be an Iron Cross in it for me.  </p>\n<p>Flicking ashes into a pelvic bone ashtray, I threw a thoughtful glance at the name on the office door: hcirdyeH .H with the abbreviated SS title of evil beneath: D.D.D., when suddenly a shapely shadow fell across the frosted glass &#8211; then a knock. </p>\n<p>Knock, knock. </p>\n<p>\u201cWho\u2019s there?\u201d </p>\n<p>\u201cIcannazi\u201d </p>\n<p>\u201cIcannazi who?\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cI cannazi any gaz chambers.\u201d</p>\n<p>It was our private joke.</p>\n<p>\u201cYeah, come in.\u201d </p>\n<p>The door opened and there she stood, deep green hair, flaming red eyes and a pair of gams any Jew would die for. Ilsa Greif, known as \u201cThe Witch of Kookenwald,\u201d was a vision of Aryan loveliness that could climb on my broomstick any day.</p>\n<p>In her usual manner, Ilsa\u2019s delicate, blanched fingers ran tantalizingly up and down the riding crop highlighting her low cut, leather ensemble before whipping it hard upon a sensuous curve of her shapely, black riding breeches. \u201cZo! How many Jews have we eliminated today Harry?\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cI don\u2019t know, I lost count after six million.\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cNo matter. I just came over to ask if you had any new tattoos today, they\u2019re running short over at the lampshade factory.\u201d    </p>\n<p>Pulling out a portfolio made from human skin, I shoved it across the desk toward the leather encased, porn queen from hell. \u201cSure M\u00e4dchen, just got these today, right before we sent the last batch over to the brain bashing machine.\u201d </p>\n<p>Picking up the nifty, but nasty notebook of Nhadzee atrocities, she riffled through the sheaves of carefully flattened tattoos. </p>\n<p>\u201cCareful with them, you know how scarce those tats are; remember tattoos are against Talmudic law.\u201d </p>\n<p>A gasp of delight escaped her blood-red lips, \u201cHarry, these are zimply wonderful and zo tasteful! You know Harry, Jews have forever claimed they were a light unto the world and now our German surgeons have made their dream come true!\u201d</p>\n<p>I felt the time was right to make my move. \u201cSweetheart, why don\u2019t we go over to the balcony shooting gallery and line up our sights on a few Juden over a beer?\u201d</p>\n<p>I could swear her fiery eyes flashed momentarily, underscoring her reply, \u201cOh Harry I\u2019d love to, but . . .\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cBut what? Its after five and we\u2019re both off the clock, as well as the charts.\u201d</p>\n<p>She batted an evil eyelash before leveling her steady gaze on the picture of Der F\u00fchrer prominently displayed on my desk. \u201cHarry, you know there is nothing I\u2019d like more than to go Juden shooting with you, but I already promised I\u2019d meet Doktor Mangeling over at the macabre medical facility to help him put schwerwasser on top of the buckets of Jewish flesh.</p>\n<p>\u201cSchwerwasser?\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cYes, you know, heavy water &#8211; to keep them from jumping around zo much.\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cSure babe. I\u2019ve heard it all before, maybe some other time.\u201d</p>\n<p>This wasn\u2019t the first time I had lost a score to the rakishly handsome doctor of death noted for legendary scalpel skills of the type myths were made from. Rumor had it Mangeling could slice open a bra strap before his unwitting victim could even think of protesting.</p>\n<p>\u201cI\u2019ve got to go Harry, Doktor Mangeling is waiting over at the licentious lab and I\u2019m already late.\u201d<br/>\n\u201cOk babe, be carful the oven door doesn\u2019t hit you in the ass.\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cYou know Harry, that\u2019s what I like best about you &#8211; your sense of humor.\u201d</p>\n<p>\u201cYeah sweetheart, I know. Like I said, I\u2019ve heard it all before.\u201d</p>\n<p>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~</p>\n<p>Tune in again next week when the makers of RJF soap bring you another episode of \u201cNhadzee Atrocities\u201d hot from Kremasign Theatre\u2019s ovens.</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"reply\"><a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/the-migrant-invasion-of-europe-get-ready-for-riots-and-the-abolition-of-the-white-race/?replytocom=948437#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( \"div-comment-948437\", \"948437\", \"respond\", \"62036\" )' aria-label='Reply to Arch Stanton'>Reply</a></div>\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n<ol class=\"children\">\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-948441\" class=\"comment odd alt depth-2 parent\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-948441\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/826921aaeb8d76d1c37f751d04887118?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/826921aaeb8d76d1c37f751d04887118?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">Dr Parker</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/the-migrant-invasion-of-europe-get-ready-for-riots-and-the-abolition-of-the-white-race/#comment-948441\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-04T14:27:00+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 4, 2017 at 2:27 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>@ Arch Stanton</p>\n<p>I feel sorry for you. I felt transforming them into a bit of humor an appropriate counterpoint to the extremely grim developments seen in that country.  </p>\n<p>This was not &#8220;cut and pasted&#8221; from my own website which, if you actually read it, has nothing to do with this subject. </p>\n<p>This is an original work created specifically for this topic. These are the very real Jewish sex fantasies that I mock in my Theater of the Absurd. </p>\n<p>Such tripe underpins the foundation of the problem. This is the reason why the majority of Germans stand silently by as Merkel and company reduce their once clean, productive country to a filthy, third world hell hole. </p>\n<p>Not too  many years ago I had German neighbor who, as an infant, suffered through the allied bombing raids. His mother immigrated to America as a war bride. Because of his mother&#8217;s influence, this man was the most obsequious Jewish supporter I have ever met in my life. In keeping with ancillary Jewish programming, he was completely enamored with the &#8220;oppressed&#8221; American Indian to whom he felt equally apologetic. As a show of solidarity with the tragic Jewish &#8220;victims&#8221;, he would fly an Israeli flag off the stern of his boat. </p>\n<p>However, he is not alone in supporting the Jews&#8217; anti-white, hate agenda.  When I was a youth of twelve, we had a German neighbor who had also survived the war and come to America as a war bride to an American solider. For some reason, and no telling where I might get such ideas, I thought it would be humorous to paint a large, orange Hakenkreuz on a blue cloth with the comment &#8220;Nazi go Home!&#8221; beneath, and tack it to her to her front door. </p>\n<p>Naturally she was incensed and hurt beyond words. Many years later, long after she had forgiven me, I learned that just before the end of the war, she had been living in a Berlin suburb. She told me that she and her young friends (she was sixteen at the time) had made a suicide pact for the moment the <a Href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xiEO-uGoHfI/VaLnvVdCDJI/AAAAAAAAWIU/DHlKa8rNzjo/s1600/Holocaust%2Brape.jpg\" rel=\"nofollow\">Soviet &#8220;liberators&#8221;</a> marched into their neighborhood.</p>\n<p>She also related how they survived by eating the rats that were overrunning the bombed out ruins in which they lived. Although the Jewish communist were a mere twelve miles away at the time, they never arrived to carry out their horrible <a Href=\"http://www.renegadetribune.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Living-torches.-Prague.-Wenceslas-Square.jpg\" rel=\"nofollow\">atrocities</a> on the innocent German people.  </p>\n<p>I have never forgotten that, while I did not act out of hatred for my neighbor, it was in fact a reflection of the Jewish hatred, played out endlessly in their media, that inspired those actions. I have lived with that thoughtless act my entire life. The memory pains me endlessly, how could I have been so callous towards my racial kin? I owe my ongoing pain to the Jews terrible, intense hatred for the German people. </p>\n<p>If western civilization is to survive, the Hallowedhoax myth must be exposed and continuously ridiculed for the lie it presented to all humanity. -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>Thanks a lot Lasha for your words. I know that things in Greece are worse than in Italy, I know that because I have contacts there due to business reasons. Local newspapers and TV do not talk about Greece anymore because 90% of italian media are embedded and their duty is to brainwash people pushing them far from the problem of the migrants. And also you have not to forget the influence of the Vatican who goes endless on repeating that we must open our hearts and our houses to our &#8220;brothers&#8221; from Africa and Middle East and that a good christian should listen to the voice and to the needs of the more desperate. Please note that in Vatican area or in their properties there is no migrant hosted.<br/>\nNow the truth is that 85/90% of migrants are males, aged from 18 to 35. They are in good physical conditions, they do not suffer hunger. Many of them come with deseases that had desappeared long time ago (tubercolosis, scabies and meningitis). When they arrive police forces cannot take their fingerprints because it offends their rights, so police has to rely on informations given by this people which nobody can control because countries of origin would not cooperate.<br/>\nAfter a first period in a center for migrants they are secretely carried with buses through the country and left them in several small or middle-sized towns where they will occupy empty buildings and later the &#8220;luckiest&#8221; will start to work for &#8220;black money&#8221; in the agriculture (10 US-dollars for 10 working hours).<br/>\nOthers will enter the circuit of drug selling, others will enter houses in the night robbing, torturing and raping. In Italy there are now many places that have become a hell. Many cities after 9 o&#8217;clock in the evening are no man&#8217;s land. Sometimes also day life is a nightmare especially for women and children living in suburb areas. We watch almost every evening in the TV cases of people that shot down thieves in the night who were robbing in their own houses. One of these shooters was accused of &#8220;excess of self-defense&#8221; because it was realized that the thief was unarmed or he was perhaps wearing a small knife. So the italian law says that the defense must be proportional to the offense. That&#8217;s really crazy!!! You imagine??? You see a thief in your bedroom and you ask him if he has a knife or a gun, you ask him what are his intentions because you have then to explain that your defense must not exceed his offense!!!!!!!<br/>\nIt&#8217;s very democratic! Don&#8217;t you think??<br/>\nOne of the shooters that shot down a thief coming from Moldova now has been convicted by the court to pay 325.000 Euros to the thief&#8217;s family.<br/>\nTwo weeks ago two gipsies were in a supermarket and they robbed some goods. They were catched by some employees of the center and locked up in a room waiting for the police. You know what happened later? The employees were accused of &#8220;illegal confinement&#8221;.<br/>\nNewspapers journalists and TV speaker cannot use the name &#8220;gipsy&#8221; or &#8220;clandestine&#8221; anymore. A new law says  these words have been replaced by &#8220;roms or sintis or nomads&#8221; and by &#8220;non european people&#8221;. Believe me, there are moments where I would like to fly away to countries like Iceland or New Zealand but I was born here and I love my country so I give my contribution to change the situation.<br/>\nThanks to everyone for the attention paid to my outburst.<br/>\nGian Franco<br/>\nItaly</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-948562\" class=\"comment even depth-3\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-948562\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a7729fbd9398763f8c3edf2110193515?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a7729fbd9398763f8c3edf2110193515?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">Winston</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/the-migrant-invasion-of-europe-get-ready-for-riots-and-the-abolition-of-the-white-race/#comment-948562\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-05T20:56:54+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 5, 2017 at 8:56 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>Thank you Mr. Spotti for the revealing view of Italy and the treachery and corruption of the Italian government. One of my Grandfathers emigrated from Italy. He was an Engineer with the rank of Captain in the Italian Army and fought against the Turks in what is now Libya or thereabouts in North Africa. His first assignment when reaching Africa was the burial of a large number of dead Italian soldiers. They died from Cholera. When he went to have his Cholera shot, he took the hint and paid &#8220;for a real one&#8221;, as they were giving shots of distilled water to all who didn&#8217;t pay. When he returned to his village in snowy, mountainous, winter in Italy the Army before honorably discharging him said: &#8220;Captain, your boots are Army issue&#8221;, and he had to walk home barefoot. Then he went to America, but returned for a few years after retirement. The kind of corruption you describe can only be addressed with very serious measures if there is no forthcoming sensible change. Pick your targets well in advance, study them, work out timing, logistics, contingency measures, whether the targets are simple economic ones or &#8230; something else. Then you can blame the deeds on immigrants and no one need be prosecuted.</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n</ol><!-- .children -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-948531\" class=\"comment odd alt depth-2 parent\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-948531\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/44949a80a6e3af20b81db86f165130bc?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/44949a80a6e3af20b81db86f165130bc?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">Pat</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/the-migrant-invasion-of-europe-get-ready-for-riots-and-the-abolition-of-the-white-race/#comment-948531\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-05T14:09:47+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 5, 2017 at 2:09 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>Gian &#8211;</p>\n<p>Good reading you &#8211; I am told the 19-minute video could be removed from YouTube any day soon. This is because of constant complaints about it from the Usual Suspects, particularly about the shockingly damning quote by Jewish activist Barbara Spectre which forms the climax of the video.\n\nGERMAN CHANCELLOR ANGELA MERKEL\n\n\u00a7 \u201cThere will be riots in Germany soon\u2026 I always thought Merkel was a great leader\u2026 [but] what she\u2019s done in Germany is insane, insane\u2026\u201d \u2014 Donald Trump in video below, 13.35 ff.\n\n\u00a7 \u201cMerkel is at the risk of an imminent mental breakdown and now represents a danger to Germany.\u201d \u2014 Hans-Joachim Maaz, top German psychiatrist and best-selling author\n\nConsumed with Holocaust guilt and possessed by the demons of pathological altruism, German Chancellor Angela Merkel has handed over her country to the endless hordes of the Third World. \u201cLet them come . . . we can look after them all,\u201d she murmurs serenely, echoing the words of the altruists all over Europe bearing placards that scream: \u201cREFUGEES WELCOME!\n\nMerkel is an interesting case history: the guilt-ridden, traumatized leader of a deeply traumatized nation. Her way of handling the migrant crisis in Germany is not so much a stupendous example of pathological altruism at work as a symbolic act of self-flagellation on behalf of the German people, all of them engaged in varying degrees of self-flagellation over the Holocaust.\n\n\u201cThe culture of the Holocaust is destroying Germany, \u201d Brenton Sanderson notes in a thought-provoking 3-part article in the Occidental Observer. \u201cEndlessly reinforced over decades by the intellectual and media elite, the notion that Germans and their descendants are responsible for \u201cthe single most evil event in human history\u201d has had such a demoralizing effect that millions fully support Angela Merkel\u2019s current attempt to destroy the ethnic basis of their nation.\u201d\n\nTo understand these words is to grasp the root cause of Germany\u2019s suicidal approach to the migrant crisis. Letting Germany be destroyed, the entire ethnic basis of the nation expunged, can be seen for what it is: a collective act of atonement for the Holocaust.\n\nI wrote this last year in an article \u2014 the situation, if anything, is even worse now:\n\nGermany has accepted roughly 1.5 million \u201crefugees\u201d last year, far more than any other country in Europe, with a predicted 4 million new asylum seekers pouring into Europe in 2016, and 10 million more on the way. Many of these will end up in Germany. At this rate, it is widely predicted, there will soon not be a single white face left in Germany\u2014or indeed anywhere else in Europe. In 50 years time, Europe will not only be multicultural, much to the delight of Jewish activist Barbara Spectre, it will also be multicolored.\n\nLast year a Muslim political activist warned the Germans: \u201cWe will marry your daughters and conquer you with births!\u201d\n\n\u201cWhat\u2019s wrong with that?\u201d you might ask if you\u2019ve been infected by the virus of pathological altruism. Well, to start with, most well-balanced Europeans don\u2019t want to see their homelands invaded by unlimited numbers of foreigners from Africa, Asia and the Middle East. They maintain, quite rightly, \u201cWe\u2019re full up, we\u2019re stuffed to capacity!\u201d\n\nIf Europe can be likened to the Titanic sinking beneath the waves, the last thing we can afford is to have more people piling on to the lifeboats.\n\n\u2014 \u00a7 \u2014\n\nHere is a Muslim on a YouTube video. Listen to his rant. You\u2019ll be hearing more talk like this soon. He\u2019s not going to kill us quickly and violently with bombs and box cutters, he\u2019s going to kill us slowly and non-violently with birth rates!\n\n\u201cI am telling you honestly, Islam will come to Germany, whether you like it or not. Your daughter will wear a headscarf (hijab). Your son will wear a beard. Okay. And your daughter will marry a bearded man. We are reproducing faster and faster. You Germans are not getting any children. In the best case, you get two children. We make seven to eight children. Okay, mate? And then we take four wives each, we have 22 children! Maybe you Germans have one child and a dog, huh? And that\u2019s it! Listen, mate. This is not our fault, it\u2019s your fault. You exploited our countries, colonized our countries. And so Allah (blessed be his name), Almighty God will make it so that we will conquer you. Not with war, here in Germany, but with birth rates, first and foremost!
